assistance from either\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        Washington\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ottawa,_Canada" title="Ottawa, Canada">\n        Ottawa\n       </a>\n       , and trying to make their case in the "court" of\n       <a href="/wiki/Public_opinion" title="Public opinion">\n        public opinion\n       </a>\n       through newspaper reporting.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY314_50-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY314-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       But other groups have entered the political process as well, including\n       <a href="/wiki/Environmentalism" title="Environmentalism">\n        environmentalists\n       </a>\n       , lakefront property owners, industry owners and workers seeking cost-effective solutions for sewage, ferry boat operators, even corporations making electric-generating wind turbines.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Management of the fishery is by consensus of all management agencies with an interest in the resource and include the states of\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">\n        New York\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">\n        Ohio\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">\n        Michigan\n       </a>\n       and the province of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ontario,_Canada" title="Ontario, Canada">\n        Ontario\n       </a>\n       , and work under the mandate of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Great_Lakes_Fishery_Commission" title="Great Lakes Fishery Commission">\n        Great Lakes Fishery Commission\n       </a>\n       . The commission makes assessments using sophisticated\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mathematical_modeling" title="Mathematical modeling">\n        mathematical modeling\n       </a>\n       systems. The Commission has been the focus of considerable recrimination, primarily from angler and charter fishing groups in the U.S. which have had a historical antipathy to commercial fishing interests. This conflict is complex, dating from the 1960s and earlier, with the result in the United States that, in 2011, commercial fishing was mostly eliminated from Great Lakes states. One report suggests that battling between diverse fishing interests began around\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Michigan" title="Lake Michigan">\n        Lake Michigan\n       </a>\n       and evolved to cover the entire Great Lakes region.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The analysis suggests that in the Lake Erie context, the competition between sport and commercial fishing involves universals and that these conflicts are cultural, not scientific, and therefore not resolvable by reference to ecological data.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Sport_fishing">\n        Sport fishing\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Sport fishing">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       The lake also supports a strong sport fishery. While commercial fishing declined, sport fishing has remained. The deep cool waters that spawn the best fishing is in the Canadian side of the lake.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX413a_110-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX413a-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As a result, a fishing boat that crosses the international border triggers the security concerns of border crossings and fishermen are advised to have their passport.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX413a_110-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX413a-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       If their boat crosses the invisible border line in the lake, upon returning to the American shore, passengers will have to "drive to a local government reporting station and pose for pictures" to Customs officers by videophone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX413a_110-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX413a-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There are cumbersome rules for fishing boat operators as well, who will have to fax passenger personal information to a government agency an hour before leaving; officers will be watching and doing spot checks from patrol boats and government aircraft".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX413a_110-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX413a-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Authorities in 2008 from the Pennsylvania Fish and Boat Commission have tried stocking the lake with\n       <a href="/wiki/Brown_trout" title="Brown trout">\n        brown trout\n       </a>\n       in an effort to build what\'s called a\n       <i>\n        put-grow-and-take\n       </i>\n       fishery.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY115_111-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY115-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There was a report that charter boat fishing increased substantially on the American side, from 46 to 638 charter boats in operation in Ohio alone, during a period from 1975 to 1985 as pollution levels declined, and after populations of walleye increased substantially in the lake.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY211_100-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY211-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 1984, Ohio sold 27,000 nonresident fishing permits, and sport fishing was described as big business.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY211_100-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY211-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 1992, there were accounts of fishermen catching 8, 10, and 12 pound walleyes, and that the "runt of a five-man daily limit of 25 walleye might be a nuisance of 5 pounds."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY212_112-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY212-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It is possible to fish off piers in winter for a fish called the\n       <a href="/wiki/Burbot" title="Burbot">\n        burbot\n       </a>\n       , also known by pseudonyms such as eelpout, mudblow, lawyer fish, cusk, or freshwater cod which looks "ugly" but tastes great; the burbot make a midwinter spawning run and is reportedly one of "Erie\'s glacial relics."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ14_99-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ14-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ice_drill.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2272" data-file-width="1704" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Ice_drill.JPG/170px-Ice_drill.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Ice_drill.JPG/255px-Ice_drill.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Ice_drill.JPG/340px-Ice_drill.JPG 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ice_drill.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         An\n         <a href="/wiki/Auger_(drill)" title="Auger (drill)">\n          ice auger\n         </a>\n         used to bore hole for ice fishing\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Ice_fishing">\n        Ice fishing\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Ice fishing">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       In winter when the lake freezes, many fishermen go out on the ice, cut holes, and fish. It is even possible to build bonfires on the ice.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY114_64-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY114-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       But venturing on Lake Erie ice can be dangerous. In a freak incident in 2009, warming temperatures and winds of 35 miles per hour and currents pushing eastward dislodged a miles-wide ice floe which broke away from the shore, trapping more than 130 fishermen offshore; one man died while the rest were rescued by helicopters or boats.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX16_113-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX16-113">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <blockquote class="templatequote">\n       <p>\n        The day began with fishermen setting down wooden pallets to create a bridge over a crack in the ice so they could roam farther out on the lake. But the planks fell into the water when the ice shifted, stranding the fishermen about 1,000 yards offshore ... When fishermen realized late Saturday morning that the ice had broken away, they began to debate the best way off. Some chose to sit and wait for authorities, while others headed east in search of an ice bridge ... Others managed to get to land on their own by riding their all-terrain vehicles about five miles east to where ice hadn\'t broken away. ... When the rescued fishermen made it to shore, authorities had them line up single-file to take down their names.\n       </p>\n       <div class="templatequotecite">\n        \xe2\x80\x94\n        <cite>\n         John Seewer, February 2009\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX16_113-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-twsX16-113">\n           [113]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </cite>\n       </div>\n      </blockquote>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sour_cherry_3428.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="225" data-file-width="300" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Sour_cherry_3428.JPG/220px-Sour_cherry_3428.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/38/Sour_cherry_3428.JPG 1.5x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sour_cherry_3428.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sour_cherry" title="Sour cherry">\n          Sour cherry\n         </a>\n         <a href="/wiki/Orchard" title="Orchard">\n          orchard\n         </a>\n         on shoreline\n         <br/>\n         at Leamington, Ontario\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Agriculture">\n        Agriculture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Agriculture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1974" data-file-width="4288" height="101" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg/220px-Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg/330px-Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg/440px-Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Lonz_Winery_6-27-10.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Winery on\n         <a href="/wiki/Middle_Bass_Island" title="Middle Bass Island">\n          Middle Bass Island\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The lake\'s formerly more extensive lakebed creates a favorable environment for\n       <a href="/wiki/Agriculture" title="Agriculture">\n        agriculture\n       </a>\n       in the bordering areas of Ontario, Ohio, Michigan, Pennsylvania, and New York. The Lake Erie sections of western New York State have a suitable climate for growing grapes, and in Chautauqua County there have been many vineyards and wineries in the area as well as in Erie County in northwestern Pennsylvania.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX42_114-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX42-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Much grape juice is produced in this region.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX42_114-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX42-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Canadian region of Lake Erie\'s north shore is becoming a more prominent wine region as well; it has been dubbed the Lake Erie North Shore, or LENS region, and includes\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pelee_Island" title="Pelee Island">\n        Pelee Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ52_115-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ52-115">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and since it is farther north than comparable wine-growing areas in the world, the season is longer in terms of light.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX415_116-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX415-116">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A longer growing season due to the lake-moderated temperatures make the risk of early frosts less likely.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX415_116-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX415-116">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The drainage basin has led to well fertilized soil. The north coast of Ohio is widely referred to as its nursery capital.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n        <a href="#cite_note-117">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tourism">\n        Tourism\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Tourism">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Diving_for_shipwrecks">\n        Diving for shipwrecks\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Diving for shipwrecks">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Lake Erie is a favorite for divers since there are many shipwrecks, perhaps 1,400 to 8,000 according to one estimate,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       of which about 270 are "confirmed shipwreck locations."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most wrecks are undiscovered but believed to be well preserved and in good condition and at most only 200 feet (61\xc2\xa0m) below the water surface.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One report suggests there are more "wrecks per square mile" than any other freshwater location, including wrecks from\n       <a href="/wiki/Indigenous_peoples_of_the_Americas" title="Indigenous peoples of the Americas">\n        Native American\n       </a>\n       watercraft. There are efforts to identify shipwreck sites and survey the lake floor to map the location of underwater sites, possibly for further study or exploration.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX28a_119-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX28a-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While the lake is relatively warmer than the other Great Lakes, there is a thermocline, meaning that as a diver descends, the water temperature drops about 30 degrees Fahrenheit change (17\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C), requiring a wetsuit.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One estimate is that Lake Erie has a quarter of all 8,000 estimated shipwrecks in the Great Lakes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       They are preserved because the water is cold and salt-free creating "intact time capsules down there".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Divers have a policy of not removing or touching anything at the wreck else the "next person won\'t be able to see it"; when artifacts were removed on occasion, it was met by "outrage" by the diving community.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cold conditions make diving difficult and "strenuous" requiring divers with skill and experience.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One charter firm from western New York State takes about 1,500 divers to Lake Erie shipwrecks in a typical season from April through October.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <blockquote class="templatequote">\n       <p>\n        Among the diving community, they are considered world class, offering opportunities to visit an underwater museum that most people will never see.\n       </p>\n       <div class="templatequotecite">\n        \xe2\x80\x94\n        <cite>\n         reporter Shannon M. Nass of the\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Pittsburgh_Post-Gazette" title="Pittsburgh Post-Gazette">\n           Pittsburgh Post-Gazette\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         , 2010\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-7">\n          <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n           [118]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </cite>\n       </div>\n      </blockquote>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="389" data-file-width="600" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg/220px-Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg/330px-Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg/440px-Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Steamship_General_Anthony_Wayne.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <i>\n          Anthony Wayne\n         </i>\n         side-wheel passenger and cargo steamship sank in 1850 but was rediscovered in 2006 by diver Tom Kowalczk about six miles (9.7\xc2\xa0km) north of Vermilion, Ohio. It is believed to be the oldest archaeological steamship wreck in Lake Erie, according to the Great Lakes Historical Society.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In 1991, the 19th-century sidewheeler\n       <i>\n        Atlantic\n       </i>\n       was discovered.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX23_120-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX23-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It had sunk in a collision with the\n       <i>\n        Ogdensburg\n       </i>\n       , a steamship sometimes referred to as a "propeller" according to 19th-century parlance, in 1852, six miles (9.7\xc2\xa0km) west of\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Point,_Ontario" title="Long Point, Ontario">\n        Long Point, Ontario\n       </a>\n       and survivors from the\n       <i>\n        Atlantic\n       </i>\n       were saved by the\n       <i>\n        Ogdensburg\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX23_120-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX23-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY315_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY315-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One account suggests 130 people drowned\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX23_120-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX23-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       while another suggests about 20 drowned.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY315_121-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY315-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The aftermath of the disaster led to calls for authorities to seize captains of both ships so "that the cause of the collision may be correctly ascertained" as well as calls for more lifeboats and improved life preservers since the earlier ones proved to be "totally useless."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsJanY315_121-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsJanY315-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There was speculation that the sunken vessel had been a gambling ship, and therefore there might have been money aboard, but most historians were skeptical.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX23_120-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX23-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 1998, the shipwreck of the vessel\n       <i>\n        Adventure\n       </i>\n       was the first shipwreck registered with the state of Ohio as an "underwater archaeological site"; when it was discovered that the\n       <i>\n        Adventure\'s\n       </i>\n       propeller had been removed and given to a junkyard, the propeller was rescued days before being converted to scrap metal and brought back to the dive site and back to its underwater home.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2003, divers discovered the steamer\n       <i>\n        Canobie\n       </i>\n       near Presque Isle, which sunk in 1921.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX28a_119-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX28a-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other wrecks include the fish tub\n       <i>\n        Neal H. Dow\n       </i>\n       (1910), the\n       <i>\n        Elderado\n       </i>\n       "steamer-cum-barge" (1880),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX28a_119-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX28a-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the\n       <i>\n        W. R. Hanna\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the\n       <i>\n        Dundee\n       </i>\n       which sank north of Cleveland in 1900,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the\n       <i>\n        F. H. Prince\n       </i>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <i>\n        The Craftsman\n       </i>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2007, the wreck of the steamship named after\n       <i>\n        Mad\n       </i>\n       Anthony Wayne was found near\n       <a href="/wiki/Vermilion,_Ohio" title="Vermilion, Ohio">\n        Vermilion, Ohio\n       </a>\n       in 50 feet (15\xc2\xa0m) of water; the vessel sank in 1850 after its boilers exploded, and 38 people died.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ37_122-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ37-122">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The wreck belongs to the state of Ohio and "salvaging it is illegal" but divers can visit it after it is surveyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ37_122-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ37-122">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, there are wrecks of smaller vessels, with occasional drownings of fishermen.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX214_123-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX214-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The finding of the well-preserved wreck of the Canadian-built British troop transport warship\n       <i>\n        Caledonia\n       </i>\n       , sunk during the War of 1812, has led to accusations about plundering of the site and legal wrangling about whether the vessel should be resurfaced in time for the 2013 war\'s bicentennial.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ42_124-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ42-124">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Research into shipwrecks has been organized by the Peachman Lake Erie Shipwreck Research Center, or PLESRC, located on the grounds of the Great Lakes Historical Society.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2008, the Great Lakes Historical Society announced plans to survey the underwater battle site of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Lake_Erie" title="Battle of Lake Erie">\n        Battle of Lake Erie\n       </a>\n       in preparation for the bicentennial celebration of the battle in 2013.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ41a_39-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ41a-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Public_parks">\n        Public parks\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Public parks">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="2871" height="142" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG/220px-PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG/330px-PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG/440px-PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:PresqueIsleStatePark.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Presque_Isle_State_Park" title="Presque Isle State Park">\n          Presque Isle State Park\n         </a>\n         is a\n         <a href="/wiki/Peninsula" title="Peninsula">\n          peninsula\n         </a>\n         that juts out into Lake Erie from Pennsylvania and is popular during summers with swimmers and beachgoers.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       There are numerous public parks around the lake. In western Pennsylvania, a wildlife reserve was established in 1991 in Springfield Township for\n       <a href="/wiki/Hiking" title="Hiking">\n        hiking\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Fishing" title="Fishing">\n        fishing\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cross-country_skiing" title="Cross-country skiing">\n        cross-country skiing\n       </a>\n       and walking along the beach.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX17_125-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX17-125">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Ontario, Long Point is a peninsula on the northwest shore near\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Rowan,_Ontario" title="Port Rowan, Ontario">\n        Port Rowan\n       </a>\n       that extends 20 miles (32\xc2\xa0km) into Lake Erie which is a stopover for birds migrating as well as turtles; one reporter found a "turtle-crossing" sign along the road;\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Point_Provincial_Park" title="Long Point Provincial Park">\n        Long Point Provincial Park\n       </a>\n       is located there and has been designated as a UNESCO Biosphere reserve.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Ontario\'s Sand Hill Park, east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Burwell,_Ontario" title="Port Burwell, Ontario">\n        Port Burwell\n       </a>\n       , there is a 450-foot (140\xc2\xa0m) high dune which is so steep it requires people to "crawl like crabs to the summit" but they are rewarded with spectacular lake views.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ35b_73-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ35b-73">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Crystal Beach, in the Village of\n       <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Beach,_Ontario" title="Crystal Beach, Ontario">\n        Crystal Beach, Ontario\n       </a>\n       , at the eastern end of the lake, is one of many South-facing beaches on the Canadian side. As such, it is perfectly situated for sun-lovers and bathers, facing the sun from sunrise to spectacular sunset. The beach is gently sloping with no sharp drop-offs or rip currents, and is usually cooled by southwest breezes, even on the hottest days.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In southern Michigan,\n       <a href="/wiki/Sterling_State_Park" title="Sterling State Park">\n        Sterling State Park\n       </a>\n       offers campgrounds, 1,300 acres (530\xc2\xa0ha) for hiking, biking, fishing, boating, with a sand beach for sunbathing, swimming, and picnicking.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ13_126-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ13-126">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Biking">\n        Biking\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Biking">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">\n         The New York Times\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       reporter Donna Marchetti took a bike tour around the Lake Erie perimeter in 1997, traveling 40 miles (64\xc2\xa0km) per day and staying at\n       <a href="/wiki/Bed_and_breakfast" title="Bed and breakfast">\n        bed and breakfasts\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       They went through the cities of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">\n        Cleveland\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Erie,_Pennsylvania" title="Erie, Pennsylvania">\n        Erie\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Windsor,_Ontario" title="Windsor, Ontario">\n        Windsor\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Detroit,_Michigan" title="Detroit, Michigan">\n        Detroit\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Toledo,_Ohio" title="Toledo, Ohio">\n        Toledo\n       </a>\n       as well as resort towns, vineyards, and cornfields.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The trip highlights were the "small port towns and rural farmlands of southern Ontario".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There are few bike repair shops in Ontario on the route.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Islands_2">\n        Islands\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Islands">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Alvar2.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="745" data-file-width="1169" height="140" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Alvar2.JPG/220px-Alvar2.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Alvar2.JPG/330px-Alvar2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Alvar2.JPG/440px-Alvar2.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Alvar2.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Lichen, moss and grasses on karstic limestone surface on\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kelley%27s_Island" title="Kelley\'s Island">\n          Kelley\'s Island\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Lake Erie islands tend to be in the westernmost part of the lake and have different characters. Some of them include:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Kelleys_Island,_Ohio" title="Kelleys Island, Ohio">\n         Kelleys Island\n        </a>\n        has activities such as beach lounging, hiking, biking, and viewing the deep\n        <a href="/wiki/Glacial_striation" title="Glacial striation">\n         glacial grooves\n        </a>\n        in the\n        <a href="/wiki/Bedrock" title="Bedrock">\n         bedrock\n        </a>\n        <a href="/wiki/Limestone" title="Limestone">\n         limestone\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX21a_21-2">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX21a-21">\n          [21]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Pelee,_Ontario" title="Pelee, Ontario">\n         Pelee Island\n        </a>\n        is reached by ferry from\n        <a href="/wiki/Leamington,_Ontario" title="Leamington, Ontario">\n         Leamington, Ontario\n        </a>\n        or by plane or ferry in\n        <a href="/wiki/Sandusky,_Ohio" title="Sandusky, Ohio">\n         Sandusky, Ohio\n        </a>\n        and is the largest of the Lake Erie islands.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-13">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n          [22]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        The island has a unique ecosystem with plants rarely found in Canada such as wild hyacinth, yellow horse gentian, and prickly pear cactus.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-14">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n          [22]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        There are two endangered snakes including the blue racer and the Lake Erie water snake. Songbirds migrate there in spring, and monarch butterflies stop over during the fall.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-15">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n          [22]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/South_Bass_Island" title="South Bass Island">\n         South Bass Island\n        </a>\n        has the island-village of\n        <a href="/wiki/Put-in-Bay,_Ohio" title="Put-in-Bay, Ohio">\n         Put-in-Bay, Ohio\n        </a>\n        which attracts young crowds who sometimes are prone to general merriment.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX21a_21-3">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX21a-21">\n          [21]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        It has been described as a party island with scenic rocky cliffs with a year-round population in the hundreds that grows during summer.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX21a_21-4">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX21a-21">\n          [21]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Surfing_The_Wind.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1752" data-file-width="2635" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Surfing_The_Wind.jpg/220px-Surfing_The_Wind.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Surfing_The_Wind.jpg/330px-Surfing_The_Wind.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Surfing_The_Wind.jpg/440px-Surfing_The_Wind.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Surfing_The_Wind.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kite_surfing" title="Kite surfing">\n          Kite surfing\n         </a>\n         is increasingly popular on the lake.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Water_sports">\n        Water sports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Water sports">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Kayaking has become more popular along the lake, particularly in places such as Put-in-Bay, Ohio.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX43d_17-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX43d-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There are spectacular views with steep cliffs with exotic wildlife and "100 miles of paddle-friendly shoreline."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX43d_17-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX43d-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Long distance swimmers have swum across the lake to set records; for example, a 15-year-old amputee swam the 12-mile (19\xc2\xa0km) stretch across the lake in 2001.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX311_127-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX311-127">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2008, 14-year-old Jade Scognamillo swam from New York\'s Sturgeon Point to Ontario\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Beach,_Ontario" title="Crystal Beach, Ontario">\n        Crystal Beach\n       </a>\n       and completed the 11.9-mile (19.2-km) swim in five hours, 40 minutes and 35 seconds, and also became the youngest swimmer to make the crossing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ33_128-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ33-128">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It is illegal for swimmers younger than 14 to attempt such a crossing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ33_128-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ33-128">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Port Dover, Ontario, brave swimmers do high-dives at the annual\n       <i>\n        Polar Bear Swim\n       </i>\n       on the beach; in 2011, the water was 32\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (0\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C), although the air was warmer, which did not deter 14-year-old youth Austin Merrell.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ23_129-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ23-129">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Currents can pose a problem, and there have been occasional incidents of drownings.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ25_130-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ25-130">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ43_131-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ43-131">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lighthouses">\n        Lighthouses\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Lighthouses">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:HPIM8229.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="1728" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/HPIM8229.JPG/170px-HPIM8229.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/HPIM8229.JPG/255px-HPIM8229.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/HPIM8229.JPG/340px-HPIM8229.JPG 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:HPIM8229.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Lighthouse on\n         <a href="/wiki/Mohawk_Island" title="Mohawk Island">\n          Mohawk Island\n         </a>\n         , Ontario\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2701" data-file-width="3784" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg/220px-Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg/330px-Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg/440px-Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cleveland_West_Pierhead_Lighthouse.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The West Pierhead Lighthouse in\n         <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">\n          Cleveland\n         </a>\n         , Ohio\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The lake is dotted by distinct lighthouses. A lighthouse off the coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">\n        Cleveland\n       </a>\n       , beset with cold lake winter spray, has an unusual artistic icy shape, although sometimes ice prevents the light from being seen by maritime vessels.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX25_132-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX25-132">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Towns_along_the_lake">\n        Towns along the lake\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Towns along the lake">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       A New York Times reporter, biking through the region in 1997, found the Ontario town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Stanley,_Ontario" title="Port Stanley, Ontario">\n        Port Stanley\n       </a>\n       to be the "prettiest of the port towns" with a lively "holiday air" but no "ticky-tacky commercialism".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Vineyards">\n        Vineyards\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Vineyards">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       There are numerous vineyards around the lake, including ones on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pelee_Island,_Ontario" title="Pelee Island, Ontario">\n        Pelee Island\n       </a>\n       which makes wines including pinot noir, riesling and chardonnay.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Summer_rentals">\n        Summer rentals\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Summer rentals">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       People can rent summer houses and cabins near the lake to enjoy the beaches, swimming, as well as be close to activities such as wine tours and fishing and water parks.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX19_133-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX19-133">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Presque_Isle_State_Park" title="Presque Isle State Park">\n        Presque Isle\n       </a>\n       is a peninsula jutting out into the lake in northwestern Pennsylvania which has nice beaches, although there were incidents in 2006 when beaches had to be closed because of unexplained unhealthy water conditions with E. Coli bacteria.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX22a_95-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX22a-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       It was described as a "spit of sand, trees and swamp that arcs off the shore" with seafood restaurants and beautiful sunsets.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX314a_23-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX314a-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Pelee Island, Canada\'s southernmost point and only three miles away from Ohio, is a place that "forces you to do nothing":\n      </p>\n      <blockquote class="templatequote">\n       <p>\n        I spent the next couple of hours riding that guy\'s creaky, brown three-speed across the flat, open island in a flawless summer breeze. I saw kilometres of gentle, swaying soybean fields. Occasional dense stands of trees. A red-brick schoolhouse attended by 10 children. A dozen cars \xe2\x80\x93 most of the drivers offering a wave. And ... that\'s about it. No stoplights. Few businesses other than a bakery, a few B&amp;Bs, a small grocery and a gift store. Certainly no chains or corporations. And that\'s the point ... excitement comes in the form of a pilgrimage to the old stone lighthouse.\n       </p>\n       <div class="templatequotecite">\n        \xe2\x80\x94\n        <cite>\n         Josh Noel of the\n         <i>\n          Nanaimo Daily News\n         </i>\n         in 2010\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ53_134-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-twsZ53-134">\n           [134]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </cite>\n       </div>\n      </blockquote>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pleasure_cruises">\n        Pleasure cruises\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Pleasure cruises">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Pleasure boat operators offer dinner cruises in the Cleveland area on the Cuyahoga River as well as Lake Erie.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ12_135-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ12-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Folklore">\n        Folklore\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Folklore">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <b>\n         Lake Erie Monster\n        </b>\n        . There have been reports of persons spotting a creature akin to the\n        <a href="/wiki/Loch_Ness_Monster" title="Loch Ness Monster">\n         Loch Ness Monster\n        </a>\n        , but there have been no confirmed reports.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX27a_104-1">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX27a-104">\n          [104]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        There were reports in 1990 of people seeing a "large creature moving in the water about 1,000 feet (300\xc2\xa0m) from their boat" described as black in color, about 35 feet (11\xc2\xa0m) long, with a "snakelike head", and moved as fast as a boat.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX27a_104-2">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX27a-104">\n          [104]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        Five other people reported seeing something similar on three separate occasions but there is no scientific evidence of such a creature.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX27a_104-3">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX27a-104">\n          [104]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        There is a\n        <a href="/wiki/Beer" title="Beer">\n         beer\n        </a>\n        named after the\n        <i>\n         Lake Erie Monster\n        </i>\n        as well as\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lake_Erie_Monsters" title="Lake Erie Monsters">\n         a hockey team\n        </a>\n        .\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX33a_136-0">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX33a-136">\n          [136]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        There were reports of people spotting a sea creature in the 19th century which was sometimes called "\n        <a href="/wiki/Bessie_(lake_monster)" title="Bessie (lake monster)">\n         Bessie\n        </a>\n        " or "South Bay Bessie".\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX33a_136-1">\n         <a href="#cite_note-twsX33a-136">\n          [136]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal,_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1500" data-file-width="2100" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal%2C_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg/220px-USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal%2C_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal%2C_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg/330px-USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal%2C_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/eb/USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal%2C_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg/440px-USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal%2C_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:USCGC_Alder_transitting_the_Welland_Canal,_on_its_way_to_Operation_Nanook_2010.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Navigating the locks in the\n         <a href="/wiki/Welland_Canal" title="Welland Canal">\n          Welland Canal\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <b>\n         Lake Erie Mirage Effect\n        </b>\n        . There have been sporadic reports of people in Cleveland being able to see the Canadian shoreline as if it were immediately offshore, even though Canada is 50 miles (80\xc2\xa0km) from Cleveland. It has been speculated that this is a weather-related phenomenon, working on similar principles as a mirage.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n         <a href="#cite_note-137">\n          [137]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Shipping_traffic">\n        Shipping traffic\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Shipping traffic">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1704" data-file-width="2272" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg/220px-Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg/330px-Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg/440px-Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sunset_over_Lake_Erie.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Sunset near a Lake Erie shipping port\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The lake has been a "bustling thoroughfare" for maritime vessels for centuries.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX15a_118-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX15a-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX28a_119-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX28a-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ships headed eastward can take the\n       <a href="/wiki/Welland_Canal" title="Welland Canal">\n        Welland Canal\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX34_138-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX34-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and a series of eight locks descending 326 feet (99\xc2\xa0m) to\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Ontario" title="Lake Ontario">\n        Lake Ontario\n       </a>\n       which takes about 12 hours, according to one source.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Thousands of ships make this journey each year.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the 19th century, ships could enter the\n       <a href="/wiki/Buffalo_River_(New_York)" title="Buffalo River (New York)">\n        Buffalo River\n       </a>\n       and travel the\n       <a href="/wiki/Erie_Canal" title="Erie Canal">\n        Erie Canal\n       </a>\n       eastward to\n       <a href="/wiki/Albany,_New_York" title="Albany, New York">\n        Albany\n       </a>\n       then south to New York City along the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">\n        Hudson River\n       </a>\n       . Generally there is heavy traffic on the lake except during the winter months from January through March when ice prevents vessels from traveling safely.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX34_138-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX34-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2007, there was a protest against Ontario\'s energy policy which allows the shipping of\n       <a href="/wiki/Coal" title="Coal">\n        coal\n       </a>\n       in the lake;\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/GreenPeace" title="GreenPeace">\n        GreenPeace\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Activism" title="Activism">\n        activists\n       </a>\n       climbed a ladder on a freighter and "locked themselves to the conveyor belt device that helps to unload the ship\'s cargo"; three activists were arrested and the ship was delayed for more than four hours, and anti-coal messages were painted on the ship.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX315_139-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX315-139">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The ship traffic in Lake Erie being the highest among the Great Lakes\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX14a_140-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX14a-140">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and roughest of the lakes has led to it having the highest number of known shipwrecks in the Great Lakes. There have been other accidents as well; for example, in 2010 according to\n       <i>\n        The Star\n       </i>\n       , crewmen from the freighter\n       <i>\n        Hermann Schoening\n       </i>\n       were sickened by\n       <a href="/wiki/Phosphine" title="Phosphine">\n        phosphine\n       </a>\n       gas which had been used to fumigate or control pests; rescuers took them by tugboat to receive medical attention.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX_141-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Ports">\n        Ports\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Ports">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <div style="width:52px">\n          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">\n           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/>\n          </a>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          This article\n          <b>\n           needs additional citations for\n           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">\n            verification\n           </a>\n          </b>\n          .\n          <span class="hide-when-compact">\n           Please help\n           <a Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.\n          </span>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (May 2017)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n          <small class="hide-when-compact">\n           <i>\n            (\n            <a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">\n             Learn how and when to remove this template message\n            </a>\n            )\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg/220px-LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg/330px-LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg/440px-LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:LakeErie_Cleveland_frozen.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Cleveland skyline in winter\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The Port of Cleveland generated over $350 million and over 15 million tons of cargo in a recent year. The current port facility is unable to handle larger cargo ships, and the cranes needed to lift goods such as steel to truck trailers are insufficient to meet current shipping standards.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Ferryboats">\n        Ferryboats\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Ferryboats">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Ferryboats operate in numerous places. But plans to operate a ferryboat between the U.S. port of\n       <a href="/wiki/Erie,_Pennsylvania" title="Erie, Pennsylvania">\n        Erie\n       </a>\n       and the Ontario port of\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Dover,_Ontario" title="Port Dover, Ontario">\n        Port Dover\n       </a>\n       ran into a slew of political problems, including security restrictions on both sides as well as additional fees required to hire border inspectors.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX314a_23-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX314a-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In particular, Canada was described as having a "sticky set of laws"; the project was abandoned.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX314a_23-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX314a-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Great_Lakes_Circle_Tour" title="Great Lakes Circle Tour">\n        Great Lakes Circle Tour\n       </a>\n       is a designated scenic road system connecting all of the Great Lakes and the St. Lawrence River.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142">\n        <a href="#cite_note-142">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One reporter thought the roads on the Canadian side were narrower, sometimes without shoulders, but were less trafficked except for the roads around the Ontario towns of\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Erie,_Ontario" title="Fort Erie, Ontario">\n        Fort Erie\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Port_Colborne,_Ontario" title="Port Colborne, Ontario">\n        Port Colborne\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Drivers can cross from the United States to the Canadian town of\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Erie,_Ontario" title="Fort Erie, Ontario">\n        Fort Erie\n       </a>\n       by going over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Peace_Bridge" title="Peace Bridge">\n        Peace Bridge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX18_22-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX18-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lake_Erie_airspace">\n        Lake Erie airspace\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Lake Erie airspace">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Golden_knights_img5.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="2958" height="138" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Golden_knights_img5.jpg/220px-Golden_knights_img5.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Golden_knights_img5.jpg/330px-Golden_knights_img5.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Golden_knights_img5.jpg/440px-Golden_knights_img5.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Golden_knights_img5.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Three US Army\n         <i>\n          Golden Knights\n         </i>\n         paratroopers linked in a tri-by-side maneuver descend to the Cleveland International Airshow.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In 2004, debris from a plane carrying 9 people was found off Lake Erie isle.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsX212_143-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsX212-143">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Border_crossings">\n        Border crossings\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_Erie&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Border crossings">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Since the border between the two nations is largely unpatrolled, it is possible for people to cross undetected from one country to the other, in either direction, by boat. In 2010, Canadian police arrested persons crossing the border illegally from the United States to Canada, near the Ontario town of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Amherstburg,_Ontario" title="Amherstburg, Ontario">\n        Amherstburg\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twsZ26_144-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twsZ26-144">\n         [144]\n
